2030:     var year = new Date().getFullYear();
2031:     var re = new RegExp('^' + prefix + '-' + year + '-(\\d+)$');
2032:     var max = 0;

2036:     });
2037:     return prefix + '-' + year + '-' + String(max + 1).padStart(4, '0');

2907: /* ===== traceability.js ===== */
2908: /**
2909:  * Sistemi Genit 6.0 — GACP-oriented end-to-end traceability for medicinal plants.
2910:  * Farm / wild collection location -> purchase -> raw lot -> processing / packaging
2911:  * -> finished lot -> delivery / sales invoice -> customer / recall.
2912:  */
2913: (function (global) {
2914:   'use strict';
2915: 
2916:   var DB = global.DB;
2917:   var C = global.Calc;
2918:   var S = global.Services;
2919:   if (!DB || !C || !S) throw new Error('traceability.js requires DB, Calc and Services.');
2920: 
2921:   function num(v) { return C.toNum(v); }
2922:   function round2(v) { return C.round2(v); }
2923:   function round3(v) { return C.round3(v); }
2924:   function nowIso() { return new Date().toISOString(); }
2925:   function clone(v) { return v == null ? v : JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(v)); }
2926:   function actor() {
2927:     var u = global.Auth && global.Auth.getCurrentUser ? global.Auth.getCurrentUser() : null;
2928:     return u || { id: 'system', username: 'system', displayName: 'System' };
2929:   }
2930:   function requirePermission(permission) {
2931:     if (global.Auth && global.Auth.requirePermission) global.Auth.requirePermission(permission);
2932:   }
2933:   function normalizeToken(value, fallback) {
2934:     var text = String(value || '').trim().toLocaleUpperCase('sq-AL');
2935:     text = text.normalize ? text.normalize('NFD').replace(/[\u0300-\u036f]/g, '') : text;
2936:     text = text.replace(/Ë/g, 'E').replace(/Ç/g, 'C');
2937:     text = text.replace(/[^A-Z0-9]+/g, '-').replace(/^-+|-+$/g, '').replace(/-+/g, '-');
2938:     return text || String(fallback || 'NA');
2939:   }
2940:   function dateOnly(value) {
2941:     var d = value ? new Date(value) : new Date();
2942:     if (isNaN(d.getTime())) d = new Date();
2943:     return d.toISOString().slice(0, 10);
2944:   }
2945:   function monthCode(value) { return dateOnly(value).slice(0, 7).replace('-', ''); }
2946:   function dayCode(value) { return dateOnly(value).replace(/-/g, ''); }
2947:   function sourceTag(value) { return String(value || '').toUpperCase() === 'WILD_COLLECTION' ? 'E' : 'K'; }
2948:   function mapUrl(lat, lng) {
2949:     if (!Number.isFinite(Number(lat)) || !Number.isFinite(Number(lng))) return '';
2950:     return 'https://www.openstreetmap.org/?mlat=' + Number(lat).toFixed(6) + '&mlon=' + Number(lng).toFixed(6) + '#map=16/' + Number(lat).toFixed(6) + '/' + Number(lng).toFixed(6);
2951:   }
2952:   function traceLocationText(x) {

2955:   }

5268:         '<td><input type="number" step="0.001" style="width:60px" value="' + l.freeQty + '" oninput="App._slLines[' + i + '].freeQty=parseFloat(this.value)||0; App.slCalc()"></td>' +

5297:   App.slCalc = function () {
5298:     let base = 0, vat = 0, total = 0;
5299:     this._slLines.forEach(function (l, i) {
5300:       const lc = C.calcInvoiceLine(l);
5301:       base += lc.baseAmount; vat += lc.vatAmount; total += lc.totalAmount;
5302:       const el = document.getElementById('sl-val-' + i);
5303:       if (el) el.textContent = App.fmt(lc.totalAmount);
5304:     });
5305:     document.getElementById('sl-totals').innerHTML = `
5306:       <div class="wf-calc-row"><span>Bazë (pa TVSH):</span><strong>${this.fmt(base)} L</strong></div>
5307:       <div class="wf-calc-row"><span>TVSH:</span><strong>${this.fmt(vat)} L</strong></div>
5308:       <div class="wf-calc-row total"><span>TOTALI:</span><strong>${this.fmt(total)} L</strong></div>`;
5309:   };

5314:   App._saveSale = async function (register) {
5315:     const customerId = SAC.getSelectedId(document.getElementById('sl-customer'));
5316:     if (!customerId) { this.toast('Zgjidh klientin', 'error'); return; }
5317:     const lines = this._slLines.filter(function (l) { return l.productId; });
5318:     if (!lines.length) { this.toast('Shto së paku një artikull', 'error'); return; }
5319:     const invoice = {
5320:       customerId: customerId,
5321:       customerName: this.data.customers.find(function (c) { return c.id === customerId; })?.name || '',
5322:       date: new Date(document.getElementById('sl-date').value).toISOString(),
5323:       dueDate: new Date(document.getElementById('sl-date').value).toISOString(),
5324:       warehouseId: SAC.getSelectedId(document.getElementById('sl-warehouse')),
5325:       paymentMethod: SAC.getSelectedId(document.getElementById('sl-method')) || document.getElementById('sl-method').value || 'cash',
5326:       lines: lines
5327:     };
5328:     try {
5329:       const saved = await S.saveSalesInvoice(invoice);
5330:       if (register) {
5331:         await S.registerSale(saved.id);
5332:         this.toast('Fatura u ruajt dhe u regjistrua! Stoku u reduktua.');
5333:       } else {
5334:         this.toast('Fatura u ruajt si konfirmuar');
5335:       }
5336:       await this.refreshAll();
5337:       this.navigate('salesList');
5338:     } catch (e) { this.toast(e.message, 'error'); }
5339:   };
5340: 
5341:   App._viewSalesList = function () {
5342:     const sales = this.data.salesInvoices.slice().reverse();
5343:     const html = `
5344:       <div class="card">
5345:         <div class="card-title">📑 Faturat e Shitjes <button class="btn btn-primary btn-sm" onclick="App._viewSalesForm()">+ Faturë e Re</button></div>
5346:         ${sales.length ? '<table><thead><tr><th>Nr</th><th>Klienti</th><th>Data</th><th>Totali</th><th>Statusi</th></tr></thead><tbody>' +
5347:       sales.map(function (inv) {
5348:         return '<tr style="cursor:pointer" onclick="App.openSaleInvoice(\'' + inv.id + '\')"><td>' + inv.docNumber + '</td><td>' + App.esc(inv.customerName) + '</td><td>' + App.fmtDate(inv.date) + '</td><td class="text-right">' + App.fmt(inv.totalAmount) + '</td><td><span class="status-badge status-' + inv.status + '">' + inv.status + '</span></td></tr>';
5349:       }).join('') + '</tbody></table>' : '<p style="color:var(--text-muted)">Nuk ka fatura shitjeje.</p>'}
5350:       </div>`;
5351:     document.getElementById('content').innerHTML = html;
5352:   };

5354:   App.openSaleInvoice = function (id) {
5355:     const inv = this.data.salesInvoices.find(function (i) { return i.id === id; });
5356:     if (!inv) return;
5357:     const linesHtml = (inv.lines || []).map(function (l) {
5358:       const lc = C.calcInvoiceLine(l);
5359:       return '<tr><td>' + App.esc(l.productName) + '</td><td>' + App.esc(l.unit) + '</td><td class="text-right">' + App.fmtKg(lc.quantity) + '</td><td class="text-right">' + (l.freeQty || 0) + '</td><td class="text-right">' + App.fmt(lc.unitPrice) + '</td><td class="text-right">' + App.fmt(lc.totalAmount) + '</td></tr>';
5360:     }).join('');
5361:     const salesSourceLinks = [];
5362:     if (inv.deliveryNoteId) salesSourceLinks.push('<button type="button" class="document-source-link" onclick="App.openLinkedDocument(\'deliveryNote\',\'' + inv.deliveryNoteId + '\')">🚚 Fletë-Dalja: ' + this.esc(inv.deliveryNoteNumber || inv.deliveryNoteId) + '</button>');
5363:     if (inv.salesOrderId) salesSourceLinks.push('<button type="button" class="document-source-link" onclick="App.openLinkedDocument(\'salesOrder\',\'' + inv.salesOrderId + '\')">🛍️ Porosia: ' + this.esc(inv.salesOrderNumber || inv.salesOrderId) + '</button>');
5364:     const body = '<div class="document-source-row"><span class="status-badge status-' + inv.status + '">' + inv.status + '</span>' + salesSourceLinks.join('') + '</div>' +
5365:       '<div class="form-grid" style="margin-bottom:14px"><div><strong>Nr:</strong> ' + inv.docNumber + '</div><div><strong>Klienti:</strong> ' + this.esc(inv.customerName) + '</div><div><strong>Data:</strong> ' + this.fmtDate(inv.date) + '</div><div><strong>Totali:</strong> ' + this.fmt(inv.totalAmount) + ' L</div></div>' +
5366:       '<table><thead><tr><th>Artikulli</th><th>Njësia</th><th>Sasia</th><th>Dhuratë</th><th>Çmimi</th><th>Vlera</th></tr></thead><tbody>' + linesHtml + '</tbody></table>';
5367:     const footer = this.standardExportMenu("App.printInvoice('" + id + "','sale')", "App.exportInvoicePDF('" + id + "','sale')", "App.exportInvoiceExcel('" + id + "','sale')") +
5368:       ((inv.status === 'CONFIRMED' || inv.status === 'DRAFT') ? '<button class="btn btn-green btn-sm" onclick="App.registerSaleDirect(\'' + id + '\')">✓ Regjistro</button>' : '') +
5369:       (inv.status === 'POSTED' ? '<button class="btn btn-red btn-sm" onclick="App.cancelSaleDirect(\'' + id + '\')">✕ Anullo</button>' : '') +
5370:       '<button class="btn btn-outline" onclick="App.closeModal()">Mbyll</button>';
5371:     this.modal('Faturë Shitjeje — ' + inv.docNumber, body, footer);
5372:   };

6289:   function addLink(out, fromType, fromId, toType, toId, relation) {
6290:     if (!fromId || !toId || fromType === toType && fromId === toId) return;
6291:     if (!CONFIG[fromType] || !CONFIG[toType]) return;
6292:     var key = fromType+':'+fromId+'>'+toType+':'+toId+':'+relation;
6293:     if (out.some(function(x){return x.key===key;})) return;
6294:     out.push({key:key,id:key,fromType:fromType,fromId:fromId,toType:toType,toId:toId,relation:relation,createdAt:new Date().toISOString()});
6295:   }

1942:   async function recordPayment(partnerType, partnerId, invoiceId, amount, method, requestKey) {
1943:     const amt=C.round2(C.toNum(amount)); if(amt<=0) throw new Error('Shuma e pagesës duhet > 0');
1944:     if(partnerType!=='supplier'&&partnerType!=='customer') throw new Error('Lloji i partnerit nuk është i vlefshëm');
1945:     const invoiceStore=partnerType==='supplier'?'purchaseInvoices':'salesInvoices', ledgerStore=partnerType==='supplier'?'supplierLedger':'customerLedger', partnerStore=partnerType==='supplier'?'suppliers':'customers';
1946:     const invoice=await DB.get(invoiceStore,invoiceId); if(!invoice||invoice.status!=='POSTED') throw new Error('Fatura e regjistruar nuk u gjet');
1947:     const payableTotal=C.round2(invoice.netAfterCredits!=null?C.toNum(invoice.netAfterCredits):C.toNum(invoice.totalAmount));
1948:     const remaining=C.round2(payableTotal-C.toNum(invoice.paidAmount));
1949:     if(remaining<=0) throw new Error('Fatura është paguar plotësisht');
1950:     if(amt>remaining+0.005) throw new Error('Pagesa tejkalon shumën e mbetur: '+remaining);
1951:     const entries=await DB.getByIndex(ledgerStore,'invoiceId',invoiceId), charge=entries.find(function(e){return e.entryType==='CHARGE';}); if(!charge) throw new Error('Nuk u gjet detyrimi');
1952:     const partner=await DB.get(partnerStore,partnerId); if(!partner) throw new Error('Partneri nuk u gjet');
1953:     const normalizedRequestKey=String(requestKey||'').trim();
1954:     const postingKey=normalizedRequestKey?'PAYMENT:'+normalizedRequestKey:'';
1955:     if(postingKey&&await DB.get('postingKeys',postingKey)) throw new Error('Kjo pagesë është regjistruar më parë.');
1956:     const now=new Date().toISOString(), currentActor=actor(), payment={id:DB.genId('pay'),partnerType:partnerType,partnerId:partnerId,invoiceId:invoiceId,amount:amt,method:method||'cash',requestKey:normalizedRequestKey,date:now,timestamp:now,createdBy:currentActor.username,createdByName:currentActor.displayName};
1957:     const txStores=['payments',ledgerStore,partnerStore,invoiceStore,'auditLogs'];if(postingKey)txStores.push('postingKeys');
1958:     await DB.atomicTx(txStores,'readwrite',function(stores){
1959:       stores.payments.put(payment);
1960:       charge.paidAmount=C.round2(C.toNum(charge.paidAmount)+amt);
1961:       const invoicePaid=C.round2(C.toNum(invoice.paidAmount)+amt), invoiceRemaining=C.round2(Math.max(0,payableTotal-invoicePaid));
1962:       charge.balance=invoiceRemaining;charge.status=invoiceRemaining===0?'PAID':'PARTIALLY_PAID';stores[ledgerStore].put(charge);
1963:       partner.balance=C.round2(C.toNum(partner.balance)-amt);partner.updatedAt=now;stores[partnerStore].put(partner);
1964:       invoice.paidAmount=invoicePaid;invoice.remainingAmount=invoiceRemaining;invoice.paymentStatus=invoiceRemaining===0?'PAID':'PARTIALLY_PAID';invoice.updatedAt=now;stores[invoiceStore].put(invoice);
1965:       if(postingKey)stores.postingKeys.put({id:postingKey,documentId:invoiceId,paymentId:payment.id,type:'PAYMENT_POST',createdAt:now});
1966:       stores.auditLogs.put(C.auditEntry('payment',payment.id,'RECORD',null,payment,invoiceId));
1967:     }); return payment;

2029:   function nextNumber(prefix, records) {
2030:     var year = new Date().getFullYear();
2031:     var re = new RegExp('^' + prefix + '-' + year + '-(\\d+)$');
2032:     var max = 0;
2033:     (records || []).forEach(function (r) {
2034:       var m = String(r.docNumber || '').match(re);
2035:       if (m) max = Math.max(max, parseInt(m[1], 10) || 0);
2036:     });
2037:     return prefix + '-' + year + '-' + String(max + 1).padStart(4, '0');

2675:   function paymentState(total, paid) {

3873: /**
3874:  * Sistemi Genit — Desktop integration facade.
3875:  * Uses the secure Electron preload bridge when available and falls back to
3876:  * standard browser downloads/printing in the Single HTML/browser version.
3877:  */
3878: (function (global) {
3879:   'use strict';
3880: 
3881:   function asArrayBuffer(value) {
3882:     if (value instanceof ArrayBuffer) return value;
3883:     if (ArrayBuffer.isView(value)) {
3884:       return value.buffer.slice(value.byteOffset, value.byteOffset + value.byteLength);
3885:     }
3886:     if (typeof value === 'string') return new TextEncoder().encode(value).buffer;
3887:     throw new TypeError('Unsupported binary payload.');
3888:   }
3889: 
3890:   function browserDownload(data, filename, mimeType) {
3891:     var blob = data instanceof Blob ? data : new Blob([data], { type: mimeType || 'application/octet-stream' });
3892:     var url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
3893:     var a = document.createElement('a');
3894:     a.href = url;
3895:     a.download = filename || 'download.bin';
3896:     a.style.display = 'none';
3897:     document.body.appendChild(a);
3898:     a.click();
3899:     a.remove();
3900:     setTimeout(function () { URL.revokeObjectURL(url); }, 2500);
3901:     return Promise.resolve({ saved: true, browserDownload: true, filename: filename });
3902:   }
3903:

3907:       return global.sgDesktop.saveBinary({
3908:         filename: filename || 'download.bin',
3909:         mimeType: mimeType || 'application/octet-stream',
3910:         data: data

5401:   App._renderProductCard = async function (productId) {
5402:     const product = this.data.products.find(function (p) { return p.id === productId; });
5403:     if (!product) return;
5404:     const movements = this.data.stockMovements.filter(function (m) { return m.productId === productId; }).sort(function (a, b) { return new Date(a.timestamp) - new Date(b.timestamp); });
5405:     let running = 0;
5406:     const rows = movements.map(function (m) {
5407:       running += C.toNum(m.baseUnitQuantity);
5408:       return '<tr><td>' + App.fmtDate(m.timestamp) + '</td><td>' + App.esc(m.sourceDocType) + '</td><td>' + App.esc(m.sourceDocNumber) + '</td><td class="text-right">' + (C.toNum(m.quantity) > 0 ? '+' : '') + App.fmt(m.quantity) + '</td><td class="text-right">' + App.fmt(running) + '</td></tr>';
5409:     }).join('');
5410: 
5411:     const html = `
5412:       <div class="card">
5413:         <div class="card-title">📦 ${this.esc(product.name)} (${product.code})</div>
5414:         <div class="kpi-grid" style="margin-bottom:16px">
5415:           <div class="kpi"><div class="label">Stoku</div><div class="value">${this.fmt(product.stock)}</div><div class="sub">${product.baseUnit}</div></div>
5416:           <div class="kpi green"><div class="label">Çmimi Blerjes</div><div class="value">${this.fmt(product.lastPrice)}</div><div class="sub">L/${product.baseUnit}</div></div>
5417:           <div class="kpi blue"><div class="label">Çmimi Mesatar</div><div class="value">${this.fmt(product.avgPrice)}</div><div class="sub">L/${product.baseUnit}</div></div>
5418:           <div class="kpi orange"><div class="label">Vlera Stokut</div><div class="value">${this.fmt(C.toNum(product.stock) * C.toNum(product.avgPrice))}</div><div class="sub">L</div></div>
5419:         </div>
5420:       </div>
5421:       <div class="card">
5422:         <div class="card-title">📊 Lëvizjet e Stokut</div>
5423:         ${movements.length ? '<table><thead><tr><th>Data</th><th>Tipi</th><th>Dokumenti</th><th>Sasia</th><th>Bilanci</th></tr></thead><tbody>' + rows + '</tbody></table>' : '<p style="color:var(--text-muted)">Nuk ka lëvizje.</p>'}
5424:       </div>`;
5425:     document.getElementById('pc-content').innerHTML = html;
5426:   };

2936:     text = text.replace(/Ë/g, 'E').replace(/Ç/g, 'C');
2937:     text = text.replace(/[^A-Z0-9]+/g, '-').replace(/^-+|-+$/g, '').replace(/-+/g, '-');

6289:   function addLink(out, fromType, fromId, toType, toId, relation) {
6290:     if (!fromId || !toId || fromType === toType && fromId === toId) return;
6291:     if (!CONFIG[fromType] || !CONFIG[toType]) return;
6292:     var key = fromType+':'+fromId+'>'+toType+':'+toId+':'+relation;
6293:     if (out.some(function(x){return x.key===key;})) return;
6294:     out.push({key:key,id:key,fromType:fromType,fromId:fromId,toType:toType,toId:toId,relation:relation,createdAt:new Date().toISOString()});
6295:   }

6667:   function positionRowActionPortal() {
6668:     var portal = document.getElementById('row-action-portal');
6669:     if (!portal || !portal.classList.contains('show') || !activeRowActionButton || !document.body.contains(activeRowActionButton)) {
6670:       App.closeRowActionMenus();
6671:       return;
6672:     }
6673: 
6674:     var margin = 8;
6675:     var gap = 5;
6676:     var buttonRect = activeRowActionButton.getBoundingClientRect();
6677:     var portalRect = portal.getBoundingClientRect();
6678:     var viewportWidth = document.documentElement.clientWidth || window.innerWidth;
6679:     var viewportHeight = document.documentElement.clientHeight || window.innerHeight;
6680:     var below = viewportHeight - buttonRect.bottom - margin;
6681:     var above = buttonRect.top - margin;
6682:     var openAbove = below < portalRect.height + gap && above > below;
6683:     var top = openAbove ? buttonRect.top - portalRect.height - gap : buttonRect.bottom + gap;
6684:     var left = buttonRect.right - portalRect.width;
6685: 
6686:     top = Math.max(margin, Math.min(top, viewportHeight - portalRect.height - margin));
6687:     left = Math.max(margin, Math.min(left, viewportWidth - portalRect.width - margin));
6688: 
6689:     portal.style.top = Math.round(top) + 'px';
6690:     portal.style.left = Math.round(left) + 'px';
6691:     portal.dataset.placement = openAbove ? 'top' : 'bottom';
6692:   }
6693: 
6694:   function focusRowActionItem(index) {
6695:     var portal = document.getElementById('row-action-portal');
6696:     if (!portal) return;
6697:     var items = Array.prototype.slice.call(portal.querySelectorAll('.row-action-item:not([disabled])'));
6698:     if (!items.length) return;
6699:     var safeIndex = (index + items.length) % items.length;
6700:     items[safeIndex].focus();
6701:   }

7115:   function downstreamRefs(type,id){var refs=[];function add(label,arr,field){var n=(arr||[]).filter(function(x){return x[field]===id;}).length;if(n)refs.push({label:label,count:n});}if(type==='purchaseRFQ')add('Porosi Blerjeje',App.data.purchaseOrders,'sourceRFQId');if(type==='purchaseOrder'){add('Pranime',App.data.purchaseReceipts,'purchaseOrderId');add('Fatura',App.data.purchaseInvoices,'purchaseOrderId');}if(type==='purchaseReceipt')add('Fatura',App.data.purchaseInvoices,'receiptId');if(type==='purchaseReturn')add('Nota Krediti',App.data.supplierCreditNotes,'purchaseReturnId');if(type==='salesQuotation')add('Porosi Shitjeje',App.data.salesOrders,'sourceQuotationId');if(type==='salesOrder'){add('Fletë-Dalje',App.data.deliveryNotes,'salesOrderId');add('Fatura',App.data.salesInvoices,'salesOrderId');}if(type==='deliveryNote')add('Fatura',App.data.salesInvoices,'deliveryNoteId');return refs;}

7133: /**
7134:  * Sistemi Genit 6.0 — UI for medicinal-plant traceability.

7142:   function num(v) { return C.toNum(v); }
7143:   function isoDate(v) { return String(v || '').slice(0, 10); }
7144:   function nowDate() { return new Date().toISOString().slice(0, 10); }
7145:   function value(id) { var e = document.getElementById(id); return e ? String(e.value || '').trim() : ''; }
7146:   function checked(id) { var e = document.getElementById(id); return !!(e && e.checked); }
7147:   function selectedId(id) { var e = document.getElementById(id); return e ? (SAC.getSelectedId(e) || e.dataset.selectedId || '') : ''; }
7148:   function escAttr(s) { return App.esc(s).replace(/'/g, '&#39;'); }

7150:   function statusBadge(status) { return '<span class="status-badge status-' + App.esc(status || 'DRAFT') + '">' + App.esc(status || 'DRAFT') + '</span>'; }

2907: /* ===== traceability.js ===== */
2908: /**
2909:  * Sistemi Genit 6.0 — GACP-oriented end-to-end traceability for medicinal plants.
2910:  * Farm / wild collection location -> purchase -> raw lot -> processing / packaging
2911:  * -> finished lot -> delivery / sales invoice -> customer / recall.
2912:  */
2913: (function (global) {
2914:   'use strict';
2915: 
2916:   var DB = global.DB;
2917:   var C = global.Calc;
2918:   var S = global.Services;
2919:   if (!DB || !C || !S) throw new Error('traceability.js requires DB, Calc and Services.');
2920: 
2921:   function num(v) { return C.toNum(v); }
2922:   function round2(v) { return C.round2(v); }
2923:   function round3(v) { return C.round3(v); }
2924:   function nowIso() { return new Date().toISOString(); }
2925:   function clone(v) { return v == null ? v : JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(v)); }
2926:   function actor() {
2927:     var u = global.Auth && global.Auth.getCurrentUser ? global.Auth.getCurrentUser() : null;
2928:     return u || { id: 'system', username: 'system', displayName: 'System' };
2929:   }
2930:   function requirePermission(permission) {
2931:     if (global.Auth && global.Auth.requirePermission) global.Auth.requirePermission(permission);
2932:   }
2933:   function normalizeToken(value, fallback) {
2934:     var text = String(value || '').trim().toLocaleUpperCase('sq-AL');
2935:     text = text.normalize ? text.normalize('NFD').replace(/[\u0300-\u036f]/g, '') : text;
2936:     text = text.replace(/Ë/g, 'E').replace(/Ç/g, 'C');
2937:     text = text.replace(/[^A-Z0-9]+/g, '-').replace(/^-+|-+$/g, '').replace(/-+/g, '-');
2938:     return text || String(fallback || 'NA');
2939:   }
2940:   function dateOnly(value) {
2941:     var d = value ? new Date(value) : new Date();
2942:     if (isNaN(d.getTime())) d = new Date();
2943:     return d.toISOString().slice(0, 10);
2944:   }
2945:   function monthCode(value) { return dateOnly(value).slice(0, 7).replace('-', ''); }
2946:   function dayCode(value) { return dateOnly(value).replace(/-/g, ''); }
2947:   function sourceTag(value) { return String(value || '').toUpperCase() === 'WILD_COLLECTION' ? 'E' : 'K'; }
2948:   function mapUrl(lat, lng) {
2949:     if (!Number.isFinite(Number(lat)) || !Number.isFinite(Number(lng))) return '';
2950:     return 'https://www.openstreetmap.org/?mlat=' + Number(lat).toFixed(6) + '&mlon=' + Number(lng).toFixed(6) + '#map=16/' + Number(lat).toFixed(6) + '/' + Number(lng).toFixed(6);
2951:   }
2952:   function traceLocationText(x) {
2953:     x = x || {};
2954:     return [x.locationName, x.village, x.municipality, x.region, x.country].filter(Boolean).join(', ');
2955:   }
2956:   function lotAvailable(lot) { return Math.max(0, round3(num(lot && lot.quantityAvailable))); }
2957:   function isSaleableLot(lot) {
2958:     return !!lot && lot.status === 'AVAILABLE' && lotAvailable(lot) > 0.0001 && String(lot.qualityStatus || 'APPROVED') === 'APPROVED';

2828:   function orderStatusAfterPurchase(order) {
2829:     var anyReceived = order.lines.some(function (l) { return num(l.receivedQty) > 0; });

2832:     return allInvoiced && allReceived ? 'INVOICED' : allReceived ? 'RECEIVED' : anyReceived ? 'PARTIALLY_RECEIVED' : 'CONFIRMED';

3334:   async function traceLot(lotId) {
3335:     var lots = await DB.getAll('lots'), lotMap = {}; lots.forEach(function (x) { lotMap[x.id] = x; });
3336:     var batches = await DB.getAll('processBatches'), inputs = await DB.getAll('processBatchInputs'), allMoves = await DB.getAll('lotMovements');
3337:     var lot = lotMap[lotId]; if (!lot) throw new Error('Loti nuk u gjet.');
3338:     function ancestors(id, seen) { seen = seen || {}; if (seen[id]) return []; seen[id] = true; var l = lotMap[id], out = []; if (l && l.outputBatchId) { inputs.filter(function (x) { return x.batchId === l.outputBatchId; }).forEach(function (x) { var il = lotMap[x.lotId]; if (il) { out.push(il); out = out.concat(ancestors(il.id, seen)); } }); } return out; }
3339:     function descendants(id, seen) { seen = seen || {}; if (seen[id]) return []; seen[id] = true; var out = []; inputs.filter(function (x) { return x.lotId === id; }).forEach(function (x) { var b = batches.find(function (y) { return y.id === x.batchId; }), ol = b && lotMap[b.outputLotId]; if (ol) { out.push(ol); out = out.concat(descendants(ol.id, seen)); } }); return out; }
3340:     var ancestorLots = ancestors(lotId), descendantLots = descendants(lotId), chainIds = [lotId].concat(descendantLots.map(function (x) { return x.id; }));
3341:     var sales = allMoves.filter(function (x) { return chainIds.indexOf(x.lotId) >= 0 && x.movementType === 'SALE_OUT'; });
3342:     var qualityChecks = (await DB.getAll('traceQualityChecks')).filter(function (x) { return x.lotId === lotId || chainIds.indexOf(x.lotId) >= 0; });
3343:     var recallCases = (await DB.getAll('traceRecallCases')).filter(function (x) { return x.lotId === lotId || chainIds.indexOf(x.lotId) >= 0; });
3344:     return { lot: lot, ancestors: ancestorLots, descendants: descendantLots, movements: allMoves.filter(function (x) { return x.lotId === lotId; }).sort(function (a, b) { return new Date(a.timestamp) - new Date(b.timestamp); }), sales: sales, batches: batches, inputs: inputs, lots: lots, qualityChecks: qualityChecks, recallCases: recallCases };
3345:   }
